both  these  activities  of  the  human  spint  For  that  reason
perhaps  more  than  for  any  other  his  teachmg  will  always  be
of  mfluence.

In  aU  judgments  wherem  the  relation  of  a subject  to  the  predicat*'

in  their  constniction
